function u9.StartColorCycle(p43, p44, p45, p46, p47)

	local u48 = 1

				["BackgroundColor3"] = v49.bg

			p47.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1, 1, 1), v49.stroke)

	end

		-- upvalues: (ref) u8, (ref) u50
		wait(u8.ANIMATION_DURATION.COLOR_CYCLE)
		u50()
	end)
	table.insert(p43.connections, v51)
	return v51
end

function u9.PlayIntroSequence(p59)

		["Size"] = u8.BLUR_INTENSITY

		["Size"] = u8.FRAME_SIZE

	p59:CreateTween(_LogoText, TweenInfo.new(u8.ANIMATION_DURATION.TEXT_FADE_IN, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
		["TextTransparency"] = 0
	}):Play()
	wait(u8.TIMING.TITLE_DELAY)
	p59:CreateTween(v63, TweenInfo.new(u8.ANIMATION_DURATION.TEXT_FADE_IN, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
		["TextTransparency"] = 0

		["TextTransparency"] = 0

		["TextTransparency"] = 1

		local v96
		v95, v96 = v93(v94, v95)

			break
		end

			v96:Cancel()
		end

local u140 = nil
local _TextChatService = game:GetService("TextChatService")
local _ChatInputBarConfiguration = _TextChatService.ChatInputBarConfiguration
if _ChatInputBarConfiguration then
	_ChatInputBarConfiguration = _TextChatService.ChatInputBarConfiguration.TargetTextChannel
end
function sendchat(p143)
	-- upvalues: (ref) _TextChatService, (ref) _ChatInputBarConfiguration
	if p143 and p143 ~= "" then
		if _TextChatService.ChatVersion ~= Enum.ChatVersion.LegacyChatService then
			if _ChatInputBarConfiguration then
				local v144, v145 = pcall(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) _ChatInputBarConfiguration, (ref) p143
					_ChatInputBarConfiguration:SendAsync(p143)
				end)
				if not v144 then
					warn("Error sending chat: " .. v145)
				end
			end
		else
			local v146, v147 = pcall(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) p143
				game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("DefaultChatSystemChatEvents").SayMessageRequest:FireServer(p143, "All")
			end)
			if not v146 then
				warn("Error sending chat: " .. v147)
			end
		end
	end
end

	["Callback"] = function(p155)
		-- upvalues: (ref) u151, (ref) u152
		local _LocalPlayer2 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
		local v157 = _LocalPlayer2.Character or _LocalPlayer2.CharacterAdded:Wait()
		local _HumanoidRootPart = v157:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local _Humanoid = v157:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
		if not u151 or u151 == "" then
			warn("No player selected for Head Sit!")
			return false
		end
		local u160 = game.Players:FindFirstChild(u151)
		if p155 then
			if not (u160 and u160.Character) then
				warn("Selected player not found or has no Character!")
				return false
			end
			_Humanoid.Sit = true
			if u152 then
				u152:Disconnect()
			end
			u152 = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) u160, (ref) _Humanoid, (ref) _HumanoidRootPart, (ref) u152
				if u160.Character and (u160.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") and _Humanoid.Sit) then
					_HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = u160.Character.Head.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, 0) * CFrame.new(0, 1.6, 0.4)
				elseif u152 then
					u152:Disconnect()
					u152 = nil
					_Humanoid.Sit = false
				end
			end)
		else
			if u152 then
				u152:Disconnect()
				u152 = nil
			end
			_Humanoid.Sit = false
		end
	end
})

						v241, v242 = v239(v240, v241)
						if v241 == nil then
							break
						end
						if v242.AssetId and tonumber(v242.AssetId) then
							_Remotes.Wear:InvokeServer(tonumber(v242.AssetId))
							task.wait(0.3)
						end
					end
					local _BodyColors = v230.Character:FindFirstChild("Body Colors")
					if _BodyColors then
						_Remotes.ChangeBodyColor:FireServer(tostring(_BodyColors.HeadColor))
						task.wait(0.3)
					end
					if tonumber(v237.IdleAnimation) then
						_Remotes.Wear:InvokeServer(tonumber(v237.IdleAnimation))
						task.wait(0.3)
					end
					local _PlayersBag = v230:FindFirstChild("PlayersBag")
					if _PlayersBag then
						if _PlayersBag:FindFirstChild("RPName") and _PlayersBag.RPName.Value ~= "" then
							_Remotes.RPNameText:FireServer("RolePlayName", _PlayersBag.RPName.Value)
							task.wait(0.3)
						end
						if _PlayersBag:FindFirstChild("RPBio") and _PlayersBag.RPBio.Value ~= "" then
							_Remotes.RPNameText:FireServer("RolePlayBio", _PlayersBag.RPBio.Value)
							task.wait(0.3)
						end
						if _PlayersBag:FindFirstChild("RPNameColor") then
							_Remotes.RPNameColor:FireServer("PickingRPNameColor", _PlayersBag.RPNameColor.Value)
							task.wait(0.3)
						end
						if _PlayersBag:FindFirstChild("RPBioColor") then
							_Remotes.RPNameColor:FireServer("PickingRPBioColor", _PlayersBag.RPBioColor.Value)
							task.wait(0.3)
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end
})
